==============================================================================
AZ'ARCH -- FULL COMPONENT SPECIFICATION
==============================================================================

Every single component of the distribution, fully expanded -- nothing
collapsed. For each package: what it is (in plain language), which
layer of the stack it sits in, what it depends on, and what depends on
it. This is the exhaustive companion to:
  - SPECIFICATIONS_COMPONENTS_OVERVIEW.svg   (the at-a-glance layered graph)
  - SPECIFICATIONS_GENERAL.md   (prose + subsystem breakdown)

The plain-language 'purpose' of each component is the official Arch
package description (the %DESC% field from the core/extra/multilib
package databases -- the same text archlinux.org and `pacman -Si` show),
with the upstream project URL. It is read straight from the package data,
so it is real and never drifts. For an interactive, clickable version of
this data, open SPECIFICATIONS_COMPONENTS_NAVIGATE_FULL.html in a browser.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
AT A GLANCE
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  Base                                       Arch Linux (rolling), x86_64
  Desktop                                    None (bare console) -- a desktop is layered on later in the overhaul
  Kernel                                     linux 7.1.4.arch1-1
  Init                                       systemd 261.1-1
  Live-session writable RAM                  4G writable overlay held in RAM
  Packages (full closure)                    916
    from core / extra / multilib             227 / 584 / 105
  Az'arch Component / Stock Arch             394 / 522
  Deepest dependency chain                   37 hops (leaf -> base)
  Total installed size                       5.15 GiB

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
HOW TO READ AN ENTRY
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  ### name (version)
  purpose:     what it is, in plain language (from the Arch package DB)
  upstream:    the project's home page
  edition:     one of --
                 az'arch  (Az'arch Component: in the set only because Az'arch added it on top of stock archiso)
                 stock    (Stock Arch: already on the stock archiso releng medium)
  category:    a single human-language role
  layer:       0 (sinks) .. 6 (leaf apps) -- real dependency depth
  requires:    the packages it directly depends on
  required-by: the packages in the set that directly depend on it
  optional:    optional deps and the capability each one adds
